Refund of Winter Grain Additional Levy: The provincial government approved the levy of seven yuan and five cents per stone for the winter grain of this county in the 18th year. At the time of collection, the county government, according to the resolution, ordered the Finance Bureau to collect an additional eight corners of silver to make up for the budget deficit. The grain households presented a telegram to the provincial government and the Department of Finance, requesting the cessation of the levy, because it had not been approved by the provincial government. The provincial government ordered the county government to refund the levy. After receiving the order, the county government issued a notice to stop the collection and refund the collected silver.

Young Girl Elopes to Demand Dissolution of Engagement: A certain Xu from a town in Qingpu is already over fifty, and his wife, Wu, has no sons under her knees, only a daughter, named Wan'e, who is 29 years old and currently studying at a girls' school in Shanghai. Xu, because he had no sons, recruited a son-in-law from Jiashan, surnamed Fang, last summer, without the consent of his daughter. But Wan'e had a lover when she was studying in Shanghai, and she had informed her father of this in a letter last winter, stating that she absolutely denied such a marriage. Xu ignored her and chose a day before to marry his daughter, decorating the house with lanterns and festoons and appearing quite busy. At this point, Wan'e knew that nothing could be done, so she suddenly took advantage of the opportunity to flee to Shanghai the day before the wedding. It is now heard that

Xu has received a letter from his daughter in Shanghai, demanding the dissolution of this autocratic marriage and the establishment of a free marriage contract. She has vowed not to return home until her goal is achieved.

Wuxi

Refugees Cause Disturbance and Are Mistaken for Bandits: Recently in the four townships within the county, there have been instances of fake refugees causing disturbances everywhere. In the Gaocheng'an area behind Yi Ba Tu outside the North Gate, at the home of the former Tu chief, Gu Guoxiang, on the afternoon of the 10th, at 2 PM, thirty to forty refugees from Funing and other counties forcibly demanded five shi of white rice. Because Gu had already been repeatedly extorted by refugees after the lean years, and had no rice left in his home, he politely refused. The refugees then caused a great disturbance in his home, smashing objects and severely beating Gu and his son, Xi'an, causing injuries. Neighbors who heard of this were indignant and tried to reason with the refugees to no avail. They then sounded the alarm, and the crowd came to Gu's home, arresting seven refugees, including Hu Tinghua and Wang Zhongkang. Gu's family had established a public school and immediately reported the situation to the nearby Provincial Farmers' Education Center. Director Chen Ruizhang reported it by telephone to the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, who relayed it to the county government. Meanwhile, patrol chief Hui Zheng was dispatched, leading police to the countryside to suppress the disturbance. After receiving the report, the county government immediately sent Zheng Chao, the first squad leader of the Third Company of the Police Brigade, leading special agent Fang Zheng and a squad of police to the countryside. They took Hu Tinghua and the other seven to the county for interrogation. At the time, it was reported in the city that bandits were causing disturbances in the countryside, causing considerable panic for a time. After the seven refugees, Hu Tinghua, etc., were brought to the county, the court interrogated them once that night and ordered that the refugees be deported.

Banning Concurrent Exchange Operations: In Zhuchang Lane outside the North Gate of this county, there are two yarn shops, Li Chang and Long Chang. Although they outwardly display yarn shop signs, their content is actually the receiving and dispatching office of a certain Lu, a broker from the Shanghai Yarn and Cloth Exchange. These two yarn shops are very accommodating in their business, so shallow-minded people flock to them. At the end of the year, many end up failing and losing heavily, even unable to make up for the losses, and stop doing business. It is undeniable that people are talking about it. Moreover, exchange brokers should conduct transactions at the exchange and are not allowed to leave the exchange, set up shops in Wuxi, and conduct private transactions. If this is not banned for a long time, it is feared that it will harm commerce significantly. Therefore, Jiang Huanqing, chairman of the Qianye Gonghui (Money Trade Association) Committee, yesterday specifically sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce, requesting that it find a way to ban it in order to maintain commerce. After receiving the letter, the County Chamber of Commerce immediately forwarded it to the two yarn shops, ordering them to quickly stop concurrently operating exchange brokerage business. It is also heard that the Shanghai-Wuxi long-distance telephone is also exclusively used by the two yarn shops, Li Chang and Long Chang, every morning, which shows the extent of their expenses.

Tragic Incident of Bomb Explosion: In front of the Wufeng Silk Factory in Zhoushanbang, this county, a Jiangbei boat was parked. The boat owner, Wang Daoquan, usually made a living as a barrel maker. On the morning of the other day, he was walking home from the street when he saw a round iron cylinder in an abandoned grave. Wang thought that it contained gold and could be melted down to obtain unexpected wealth. He immediately returned to the boat and placed the iron cylinder in a pot to melt it. Unexpectedly, the iron cylinder caught fire and exploded with a loud noise. Wang Daoquan's face, legs, and other parts were severely injured. Later, a passerby sent Wang to Puren Hospital for treatment.

Farmers' Bank Holds Business Discussion Meeting: After the establishment of branch offices of the Farmers' Bank in various counties of Jiangsu Province, a business discussion meeting was held at the Wuxi branch in Houzhuchang Lane in Wuxi on the 10th. The directors and heads of the seven branch offices in Changshu, Wujiang, Gaochun, Songjiang, Wujin, Kunjiang, and Wuxi attended. The meeting began at 10 AM. The attending directors and heads of various counties reported in sequence, mainly on four items: deposits, loans, remittances, and the organization of cooperatives.

Two Companies Compete to Open Shuttle Boats: From Anting Station on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway to Taicang, the Taixing Company has been operating shuttle boats, and the business is not bad. Recently, the Louqin Company has started to compete with it on the same route. Taixing, considering that it spent a lot of money on rebuilding bridges and dredging waterways along the way when it first started operating, is willing to share the cost and extend the route to Shantou for joint operation. Louqin has not yet agreed. Now, Taixing has filed a complaint with the county government, arguing that Louqin's pier at the station is behind its pier, and passengers must pass through Taixing's pier to disembark, which inevitably infringes on Taixing's sovereignty. County Magistrate Chen has ordered the district office to stop it.

The other seven seemed to be suspects. Squadron Leader Chen will wait to retrieve the firearms from the river before transferring them to Battalion Commander Chen Gang to be sent to the county for interrogation.

Jiangyin

Murder for Money Case at Tangjia Bridge: Wu Rukang, a farmer from Tangjia Bridge, Tenth Bao, Qiaoqi Township, ran a noodle shop for a living. At the beginning of the old lunar year, the villagers, following the usual practice, held a Buddhist festival at Diaoyudun, about two li from the village. On this day, Rukang, along with the village elders, also went to participate. At around 6 PM on the 9th, after dinner, he was going home when he was suddenly stopped by Wu Xigen, who was watching over the Diaoyudun Buddhist festival, along with Wu Xirong, Wu Bingquan, Xia Aliu, and three other people. They blocked his way at Miaohangtou, about one li from Diaoyudun, and killed Rukang with a knife. They also robbed him of all 167 yuan of public funds divided from the Buddhist festival. His leather mandarin jacket, cotton robe, and cotton-padded jacket were also stripped off. They fled and scattered with the stolen goods. Unexpectedly, although Rukang had fainted at the time, he gradually regained consciousness and crawled to the home of Tang Rupei, a hired worker half a li away, and then fainted. Rupei called back Zou You and carried Rukang to his home for urgent treatment. His consciousness gradually cleared, and his mother, Wu Gu, asked him about the situation. He soon died of exhaustion. Wu Xigen and Wu Xirong were captured. Personnel were dispatched to the countryside to verify and bring the murderers to the city for interrogation and detention.

Robbing Property but Not Admitting Robbery: Wu Houzai from Xiagang opened a wood shop east of the bridge. At 12 PM on the sixth night of the old lunar year, when the men and women in the house were asleep, six or seven bandits suddenly broke into the house, searched extensively, and plundered away, losing 120 yuan in cash. Because Lu Shengrong, the son of Lu Fulin from Lujiatang, was among the robbers, he reported it to the public security station, which detained Lu Shengrong and sent him to the Fifth Sub-Bureau for interrogation. He did not admit to the robbery. On the 10th, he was sent to the General Bureau. After being interrogated by Director Zhang, he claimed that he had an urgent need the year before and sold the two fen and two li of ancestral homestead to Lu Chaolin. Lu Fulin dug up the foundation of the wall for no reason. He reported it to the police station and went to arrest him. Lu Fulin and Wu Houzai are relatives, so they have a grudge and falsely accused him of being a robber. After the interrogation, he was sent to the county for handling.

Finance Department Urges Payment of Taxes: The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance believes that the budget revenue of this province, apart from land tax, is only the deed tax. In addition to ordering the tax inspectors of rice, fish, pigs, etc. to investigate and clarify the amount of rice, fish, pigs, and other taxes collected by the various bureaus and offices before the end of January, as well as the 10% to 20% surcharges, and fill in the forms separately, they also issued an order to the various county tax bureaus to quickly pay in full the deed tax collected and stored before the end of January of this year and hand it over to the inspectors for use.

Chairman Niu is About to Return to the Province: Niu Yongjian, the chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, stayed in Shanghai for illness for many days. It is now heard that Niu's brain disease has gradually recovered, and he is scheduled to return to the province on the 15th of this month to take office. The staff in the government are preparing everything.

Yangzhou

Yangzhou-Huogou Road is About to Start Construction: According to the plan submitted by Wang Daonian, the director of the Jiangdu Construction Bureau, the Jiangsu Construction Department requested to build the Yangzhou-Huogou and Yangzhou-Yi roads first. Yesterday (the 9th), it specifically instructed the Construction Bureau to approve the construction of the Yangzhou-Huogou Road first and to report the start date in advance. It is heard that the Construction Bureau has not yet completed certain arrangements, and it is difficult to set a date for the start of construction.

Warranted Wang Company Commander Who Was Falsely Accused: Wang, the company commander of the Fourth Company of the Fourth Battalion of the Huainan Anti-Smuggling Force, was previously falsely accused by bandits, and the Provincial Public Security Team detained him and kidnapped 19 soldiers. Wu, the battalion commander of the battalion, has telegraphed Director Tang of Anti-Smuggling, who relayed the telegram to the provincial authorities, stating the circumstances of the false accusation. He was ordered to be acquitted and released back to the battalion for work.

School Opening and Salary Demands: The funds for various schools in this county have only been paid 70% of the amount up to the end of the old lunar year. The schools originally planned to start school on February 16, but the teachers required the Education Bureau to fully pay the remaining 30% of the funds for December and the full amount for January before they would agree to teach. Today (the 10th), more than ten teacher representatives went to the bureau to ask for instructions. It is heard that Director Ling promised to do his best to find a way, and although the January funds cannot be paid as scheduled, the 30% for February will be paid off before the start of school no matter what. The representatives believed that this was not to the point and discussed for a long time without any results. It is heard that the teachers and staff will hold another meeting tomorrow to discuss the above two issues.

Recent News on the Preparation of the County Court: The Jiangdu County Court was initially unable to be established as scheduled due to financial difficulties, although the Higher Court repeatedly set deadlines for its establishment. However, the court site (i.e., the office of Ganquan County) could not be done without 4,000 or 5,000 yuan. Recently, it was heard that the Higher Court specially sent Secretary Shi Peisheng to Yangzhou to prepare for the establishment, planning to convene various public organizations today to hold a meeting for discussion and raise funds for repairs. Once the construction is completed, it will be established immediately.

Qingjiang

Bandits Pretend to Enlist Laborers to Carry People: The area around the west side of Xiba Town is relatively remote. Outside the gate of the old Gongmao Salt Shop, two soldiers from the salt transport escort team were stationed to guard it. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the 5th, more than ten bandits, including two bandits disguised as soldiers wearing military uniforms and carrying long guns, and the remaining bandits wearing long robes with pistols hidden inside, first went to the shop gate to notify the guards, falsely claiming to enlist laborers to come here, hoping not to be mistaken. They then entered the shop one after another to Li Lifu's home and demanded money from Lifu while robbing Li's wife of two gold rings, a gold ear pick, a gold hairpin, and other valuables. Then, they kidnapped Li's nephew, Ding San. At that time, Li was at home, hiding in a remote place to avoid being kidnapped by the bandits. When the bandits entered the shop, they left one bandit outside, pretending to talk to the guards. Then, they robbed the guards of their guns. On the 7th, the county magistrates of Huaiyin, Huai'an, Lianshui, Siyang, and Shuyang discussed the joint defense measures for the five counties at the Huaiyin County Government. Originally planned as a joint meeting, it was changed to a discussion meeting because of the small number of people. Generally based on the previous meeting methods of Huai'an, Huaiyin, and Lianshui, the long-distance telephone and automobile of the five counties were seriously reorganized. If there is a bandit alarm in the border area between the two counties, they must work together to suppress it. If bandits from County A flee to County B, they can go to suppress them to avoid paperwork. As for the joint defense command, it will be postponed temporarily to save costs.

Jinggong

Reed Tax and Acre Donation Cannot Be Reduced: At the county government meeting the other day, it was resolved that the five-fen acre donation for road construction should also be reduced to one-half because the reed tax was half of the ordinary cultivated land. It was reported to the Construction Department. Now, the instruction said that there was no such clear provision in the original case, and the unauthorized reduction was extremely inappropriate, and the request was not approved. 1

Trial Staff Promoted to Judge: Trial staff Wen Zheng was ordered by the Ministry of Justice to be appointed as a judge of the Huzhou District Court in Zhejiang. He must go to his post soon. The vacant position will be temporarily held by Zhang Yizhi, a member of the Case Clearance Committee.

Swearing at Bandits for Urinating Results in a Fine of 15 Yuan: There were bandits in front of Guangling Town urinating on the riverbank. The mother of Zhang Meisheng, who lived next to the old stove, cursed at them for obstructing water collection. The bandits knew about it, and in anger, wanted to burn down the house. After mediation, they were paid 15 yuan before they stopped.

Nantong

Gangs Rampant at the Junction of Tongzhou and Rugao: At places such as Zhentao Silk and Yugang at the junction of Nantong and Rugao counties, more than a thousand bandits gathered and a riot occurred. On the 6th, they harassed. On the morning of the 10th, the police team of Tong County and the defense corps intercepted more than 30 bandits in Pingchao and escorted them to Tongzhou by car that night.

Counties in Jiangbei Continue to Recruit Laborers: At the end of last year, the counties in Jiangbei were ordered by the province to stop recruiting laborers for road construction. On the 10th, they were ordered by the Provincial Government to plan and build highways and recruit laborers as soon as possible.

Joint Defense Office Investigates Bandit Collusion Case: According to the confessions of bandit leaders Qiu Hekun and Tang Haitao, Zhang Jianqing of Tangzha District was involved in many cases. Zhang was arrested and investigated.

Five Bandits Killed in Dongxiang: A bandit riot occurred in Dongxiang on the 9th. The bandits Zhang Jinsheng, Wu Elin, Wang Weixin, Yu Yigui, and Yu Daode were captured and were being escorted by the team. The bandits followed to try to seize them. The police killed the five bandits.

Implement Reorganization of Granaries: The Civil Affairs Department appointed Gu Naijun to come to Nantong and, together with the County Government, reorganize the granaries. Representatives from various organizations and agencies were convened to hold a meeting to decide on the reorganization method and to elect Zhang Xin'yu, Xu Hanru, Cai Guohua, Li Yinong, and Sun Jing as members of the granary management committee.

Huzhou

Lake Bandits Run Rampant in the Western Countryside: Although the large groups of Lake Bandits still escaped to Taihu after being jointly suppressed by the Jiangzhe Water and Land Army and Police, there are still quite a few in the territory of Changxing County. It is now heard that at about 1 PM on the afternoon of the 6th, three large boats suddenly came to Yaojiaqiao, Changxing County, which belongs to Huzhou. There were more than 50 bandits on each boat, holding pistols, Mauser pistols, and other weapons. The villagers were extremely panicked when they saw them. The bandits told the villagers, "We are robbing the big places of Wuzhen. This is a small place, and we will definitely not disturb you. Don't be afraid." At that time, seven or eight bandits went to a certain grocery store north of the bridge. It happened that guests were having lunch and fled when they heard that the bandits had arrived. The bandits drank the remaining banquet wine and left a five-yuan bill as payment. They also robbed five civilian boats in the river by the bridge. After the incident, the Changxing County Government heard the news and immediately ordered the security team to rush to suppress and capture them. The bandits had already escaped towards Chongyanggang.

The Steamship Bureau Requests Exemption from Donation: The Wuxing County Government in this city ordered from the province that from January this year, the steamship bureaus should pay 10% of the donation. The 20 steamship bureaus in the city, including the city chiefs Hang Yuantong, jointly submitted a request to the County Government, saying that the steamship business in Huzhou was sluggish and it was actually impossible to pay the donation. Therefore, they planned to forward the request to the Provincial Government for exemption in order to maintain the commercial difficulties.

Hangzhou

Two Zhejiang Bandits Have Been Captured: The notorious bandit Zhou Ami, who ran rampant in Anji, Xiaofeng, and other counties, was captured by the First Company of the Second Battalion of the Second Regiment of the Security Team at Chen Ergu's home in Wayao, Xiaofeng. Chen Ergu was also detained and will be executed by firing squad in accordance with the law on punishing bandits. The province was telegraphed yesterday to ask for instructions. Another notorious bandit, Guo Laosan, from Pingqiao, Changxing, has committed more than 20 major robbery cases. The Jiaxing Chinese robbery case was also committed by Guo. He has now been captured by the Security Team and confessed to the Second Regiment. He will be sent to the province in the coming days.

Provincial Government Sends Troops to Defend Against and Suppress Fujian Bandits: The Zhejiang Provincial Government received reports that more than 1,000 Fujian bandits were planning to rob the county seat of Jingning County in Chuzhou. Military police were stationed to defend against and suppress them, and many kinds of evidence of the riot were found. Although it is now calm as usual, the military strength is weak and it is not a way to protect the territory. Zhu Siming, the director of the Security Department, was ordered yesterday to send heavy troops to guard the key points near the Fujian border.

Hangzhou-Pingyao Highway Officially Opens to Traffic: The Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau expects that the entire line of the Hangzhou-Pingyao Highway will be completed by the 13th of this month. Yesterday, it specifically instructed to rush to complete the traffic procedures and officially sell tickets for passengers on the 15th of this month.

General Chamber of Commerce to Implement Reorganization: The Hangzhou General Chamber of Commerce believes that the Chamber of Commerce Law has been promulgated and should be reorganized as soon as possible. It held a preparatory meeting yesterday afternoon to discuss all the proceedings. It is heard that it has also been decided to implement the election and reorganization on the 15th of this month.

City and County Officially Divide the Region: The matter of dividing the area between the city and county has been discussed and decided by Zhou Xiangxian, the mayor of Hangzhou, and Pan Zhongjia, the magistrate of Hangzhou County. The urban area will still be divided into six districts as stipulated in the capital, and the county area will be reduced in scope and also divided into six districts: 1) Diaoqin District, 2) West Five District, 3) Gaoqiao District, 4) Middle Four District, 5) Linping District, 6) Pingyao District. The Civil Affairs Department will send personnel to re-survey and file for record in the coming days.

French僑 Requests Direct Consultation Rights: The French Consul General stationed in Shanghai requested the Hangzhou Municipal Government to retain the right to direct consultation because the 交涉署 (Negotiation Bureau) was abolished. The Municipal Government replied to the Consul yesterday in accordance with the post-disaster settlement measures for reference.

Ningbo

Municipal Government Ships Guns: The Ningbo Municipal Government purchased 32 Browning guns and 50 Mauser pistols from Shanghai to consolidate defense. They were shipped by boat on the 8th of this month. Personnel were sent by the Municipal Government to take them back for distribution and use.

Major Fire on Jiangxia Sugar Trade Street: In Ningbo City, a fire broke out in the attic of Tonghetai Nanhua Exchange Shop on Jiangxia Sugar Trade Street at around 3 AM yesterday (the 9th). The fire suddenly flared up. The water dragon societies and fire brigades rushed to the scene to rescue. The fire was extinguished at around 5 AM. It is estimated that four buildings of Tonghetai were burned down, with a loss of about 12,000 yuan. Five buildings of the Shenyu Qianzhuang (Money Shop) next door were burned, with a loss of 2,500 yuan. After the fire was extinguished, the police from the First Branch of the First District sent police to summon Qian Pintang, the manager of Tonghetai, as well as the leaders Wu Xinrong and apprentice Bao Hegeng for interrogation. The officer of the branch believed that the cause of the fire was unknown. In addition to ordering Wu and Bao to wait for trial and re-summoning them, he sent Qian Pintang to the Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Letter

Letter from Xu Liansheng of Pinghu

Respectfully, in your newspaper on the 2nd of this month, in the local correspondence column on the third page, there was a report that Xu Zhiting of Pinghu was shot and killed by bandits. I was very surprised when I read it. Zhiting is the younger brother of Liansheng, and he runs a rice business. Because the Pingyi Rice Industry Association has a security corps, he has military knowledge for self-defense. Unfortunately, last winter, he and his comrades Wang Jinfu and others went to Shengze Town to visit friends. It happened that the Taihu bandit party was rampant there. He was recruited by Captain Ma of the Jiangsu Water Police to suppress the bandits. Zhiting and Wang Jinfu and others were fearless for a while and died in battle in Hengtang. Now, the aftermath is still being negotiated. As for Zhiting's life, he was a formal businessman and did not sell salt or gamble. His death was actually in battle against the bandits. The report in the newspaper is not consistent with the facts. I would like to 陈情 and ask you to correct it. Xu Zhensheng of Pinghu.

National Education Conference

Situation of the First Preparatory Meeting

Yesterday (the 10th), at 2 PM, the preparatory committee for the National Education Conference held its first preparatory meeting in the Ministry of Education's conference room. Attendees included Chen De-zheng, Zhu Jing-nong, Gu Shu-sen, Jiang Shao-mo, Zhao Ting-wei, Chen He-xian, Zhao Nai-chuan, Chen Jian-xiu, Liu Da-bai, Yang Fang, Yu Wen-can, and Huang Jian-zhong. Discussion of the National Education Conference budget; 4. Discussion of methods for accommodating members; 5. Nomination of section secretaries for this committee; 6. Other matters. (Resolutions) 1. After the meeting, the chairman reported, stating that the proposals for this National Education Conference will be drafted separately by the Education Program Committee. Attending members cannot freely propose motions, which is slightly different from the National Education Conference convened during the former University Council era. Currently, all programs are being organized separately, and the conference date is not far off. Various meeting matters need to be urgently discussed and decided. Today, everyone was specially invited to the Ministry to hold the first meeting of the National Education Conference Preparatory Committee. 2. The draft regulations for the National Education Conference were amended and passed article by article, to be promulgated and implemented after approval by Minister Jiang. 3. The draft budget for the National Education Conference has not been completely decided. 4. Accommodation of members will be divided into four areas: Shanghai, Pukou, Xiaguan, and the inner city, with each area responsible for its respective arrangements. 5. Section secretaries for this committee were nominated by the respective section heads and approved through discussion, as follows: Accommodation Section Head: Zhu Jing-nong; Secretaries: Gao Xing, Zhu Shu-sen, Guo Lian-feng, Zhang Bang-hua, Lou Sheng-quan, etc.; Administration Section Head: Jiang Shao-mo; Secretaries: Rong Wei-yang, Shi Wei, Wu Lü-bing, Zuo Jin-duo, Zhu Shu-sen, etc.; Documentation Section Head: Zhao Nai-chuan; Secretaries: Zhou Gan, Zhang Ying-ming, Dai Ying-guan, Chen Zhe, Xu Xu-dong, etc.; Editing Section Head: Huang Jian-zhong; Secretaries: Wu Yan-yin, Zhao Ting-wei, Guo You-shou, Shu Chu-shi, Wang Feng-tong; Accounting Section Head: Yu Wen-can; Secretaries: Zheng Yang-he, Qi Bang-ji. The meeting adjourned around 5 PM. Detailed meeting minutes will be published after being organized.

Ministry of Education Circular Regarding Points to Note for Church Schools

Order to Strictly Investigate and Immediately Ban

Yesterday (the 10th), the Ministry of Education issued a circular to the education departments of all provinces and special municipalities, ordering them to strictly investigate the points to be noted for church schools established by religious organizations and to report them at any time. The original order is recorded as follows:

It has been ordered that private schools established by religious organizations must not engage in religious propaganda, nor may they make religious subjects compulsory. Now, it is approved to order each (department) [bureau] to strictly investigate the following points for unapproved church schools: 1. Whether Party ideology education is being implemented, and whether all Party ideology teachers and training directors have been certified as qualified; 2. Whether middle and high schools have followed regulations by not making religious subjects compulsory, and whether there are any malpractices such as forcing students to take elective courses; 3. Since elementary schools do not have elective courses, whether there are any situations where children are required to study religious subjects under the guise of electives; 4. Whether there are any instances of students being forced to participate in religious ceremonies outside of class. If any of the above situations are found, they should be immediately banned to emphasize education and protect national character. This is the order.

Ministry of Education Stipulates Regulations for Science Consultation Offices

All Academic Institutions Willing to Comply

(Central News Agency) The methods for establishing science consultation offices in various regions were previously proposed by the Shanghai Special Municipality Party Department and submitted to the Central Government, which instructed the Ministry of Education to formulate methods and send letters to the Academia Sinica, Peking Research Academy, universities, specialized schools, and academic organizations to comply. Replies have been received from various locations agreeing to comply. The China Science Society is willing to sincerely answer questions in the Science Monthly. The stipulated methods are as follows: 1. The office shall be named Science Consultation Office. 2. The office is established to answer all difficult scientific questions. The office will do its best to answer consultations on various specialized scientific fields. 3. In addition to being established in the Academia Sinica, the office will also be established in various universities, specialized schools, and scientific organizations. 4. Faculty members of universities and specialized schools and members of academic organizations have the obligation to answer all specialized questions. When necessary, a majority of faculty members or members may jointly answer the questions. 5. Consultants should forward their questions through the organization or group to which they belong, such as students through schools, and businessmen through chambers of commerce. The office may also answer questions from individuals who study science privately and do not belong to any organization or group, depending on the circumstances. Answers to important scientific questions may be published by the consultation office at any time.

Local News

Twenty-One Organizations Host Farewell Party for Party Members Studying Abroad

Chen De-zheng, Cai Yuan-pei, Zhu Shao-ping, Hu Shu-hua, and Others Give Speeches

The Shanghai Special Municipality Education Bureau, World's Chinese Students' Federation, Jiaotong University, Central University Business School, Health Construction Committee, Shanghai County Education Bureau, China Science Society, National Jinan University, Qixiu Girls' School, National Tongji University, China Critic Weekly, Medical Review Society, Commercial Press, Sino-French Industrial School, Fudan University, Sino-French Medical School, Zhonghua Book Company, Shen Bao, Shanghai Morning Post, National Labor University, Overseas Chinese Coordination Association, and other twenty-one organizations held a meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:30 PM in the Hua'an Building on Jing'an Temple Road to bid farewell to Party members selected by the Central Government to study abroad. Approximately one hundred people attended, including Cai Yuan-pei, President of the Academia Sinica, Leng Jun, Shanghai County Magistrate, Chen De-zheng, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau, and representatives from various organizations. First, the Party members studying abroad and the attendees took a group photo as a souvenir. A tea party was then held, with Chen De-zheng, Director of the Education Bureau, presiding. The chairman's speech briefly stated that he, representing the farewell organizations, respectfully extended his best wishes to everyone. The comrades were leaving to study abroad, and great hopes were placed on them, as China was backward in all aspects and had to learn from others to ensure the survival of the nation. The comrades were going far across the ocean to seek advanced studies, which was of great importance to the Party and the nation. However, the value of knowledge depended on the individual. In the world, those who accomplished great things were those with great knowledge, but also those who committed great evils, all of whom possessed great knowledge to achieve their evil. He hoped that the comrades would return with useful knowledge to meet the needs of the country. In the past, those who went abroad to study often could not be used after returning, and even harmed the country, wasting huge sums of money, which was truly heartbreaking. The reason for this was the government's neglect of this matter. Now, the Central Government has selected outstanding young people from across the country, who are knowledgeable and experienced, and will not fail the expectations of the Central Government when they return. Only a few years will pass quickly. When everyone returns in the future, the farewell organizers will surely watch the achievements of the comrades with anticipation, so work hard. Next, Cai Yuan-pei, President of the Academia Sinica, gave a speech, stating that the Party members selected by the Central Government to study abroad had a considerable history of working for the Party. Sending them abroad was to compensate for the losses they had suffered by suspending their studies to work for the revolution. However, the motivation for comrades to pursue advanced studies this time was their own. Therefore, it can be analyzed as follows: 1. Subjectively, to achieve their own goals. 2. To enrich the domestic education level by seeking advanced studies abroad. Therefore, the goal of going abroad is to study, which is also to prepare in advance to serve the Party and the nation. Furthermore, research work is a characteristic of foreign universities. The comrades must first set their own standards for study and engage in advanced research so that they can return with a clear conscience in the future. Following this, speeches were given by Leng Jun, Shanghai County Magistrate, Zhu Shao-ping of the World's Chinese Students' Federation, Hu Shu-hua, President of Tongji University, and Wang Ke-ren, a member of the Management Committee. Magistrate Leng said that China cannot close itself off from the world, and that at a minimum, it must keep pace with other countries in all aspects. Studying abroad is to make up for our shortcomings with the strengths of others. Furthermore, to build a new China, there must be people with the ability to build it. The comrades are going abroad to study with a great responsibility. Zhu Shao-ping described the points to note when studying abroad, that they should be careful with their luggage and travel, and should travel and stay abroad more. Hu Shu-hua briefly said: 1. He hopes that the comrades will do more publicity work abroad so that foreigners can understand the truth about our country. 2. They must seek knowledge in a practical way and not value gaining false fame. Wang Ke-ren briefly said that the issue of studying abroad is worthy of study. Those who went abroad to study in the past were often unaware of the social conditions in their own country, and could not put what they learned into practice after returning. However, this time, the Central Government has selected comrades who are ideologically aligned and will surely benefit the Party and the nation when they return. Finally, Cao Li-ying, the representative of the Party members studying abroad, gave a reply and thanked everyone before the meeting was adjourned.

Also, a total of forty-six Party members were selected to study abroad this time. The previous report omitted Wang Muzun. Wang Muzun is from Yancheng, Jiangsu Province. He graduated from the Central Academy of Sciences and served as a political instructor for the 6th and 10th Armies of the National Revolutionary Army. He now plans to go to the University of Edinburgh in the United Kingdom to specialize in politics and education. This is especially added here. Furthermore, a discussion meeting will be held at the World's Chinese Students' Federation at No. 95 Carter Road this afternoon at 3 PM.

Newly Approved Private Schools by the Municipal Education Bureau

Four Schools Approved... One School Banned

Director Chen of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau pays close attention to private schools in the city. Recently, private schools have applied for approval and have been approved. These include the Shanghai Baptist University Affiliated Middle School, Fudan University Affiliated Middle School, Youmin Elementary School, Xiude Elementary School, and Kindergarten, totaling four schools. Furthermore, the private Pujiang Middle School on Hart Road has no foundation and no responsible school board. Most of the teachers are part-time, which does not comply with the regulations for private schools and is detrimental to young people. It has been ordered to close and liquidate its finances, and to issue certificates to students to facilitate their transfer to other schools.

The 20th of This Month

▲Women's Tournament to Be Held After Men's Tournament

▲Chinese Team Already in Preparation

The upcoming Shanghai International Basketball Tournament and the unprecedented Women's International Basketball Tournament have been discussed and planned by the Shanghai Basketball Association Committee at a meeting held last night at the Xinbanjiu Zhai. These events are expected to materialize in a month. The committee members are Bei Zuguang, Rong Qizhao, Ma Detai, Wu Bangwei, Xu Zhendong, and Le Xiurong. Those who attended last night were Lin, Ma, Wu, Le, and Hao Boyang from the Association for the Advancement of Collaboration, totaling seven people. The committee members discussed the two international basketball tournaments in detail, and the results were very satisfactory.

Applications for the Men's International Basketball Tournament will open today, and the tournament is scheduled to open on March 1st. It has been decided to invite Zhang Guoxun, Shu Hong, Xu Zhendong, and Shu Hong to serve as referees. The players for the Chinese team will be selected from various teams, and Ma Detai and Song Junfu will be appointed as coaches.

The Women's International Basketball Tournament will be held after the closing ceremony of the Men's International Tournament, around March 15th. The Chinese team will be selected from the Jiangnan and Liangjiang Liuxing teams, and Li Feiyun will be appointed as coach. Wu Bangwei, Shu Hong, Shao Ji, and Smith will be invited to serve as referees for the tournament.

Minutes of the Chinese Sports Referee Meeting

Resolution to Recruit New Referees

The monthly meeting of the Chinese Sports Referees Association was held yesterday at the same time as the International Basketball Committee meeting. After the president, Wang Yuandao, announced the opening of the meeting, Le Xiurong proposed that the current number of referees is not enough and that it is necessary to cultivate talent to meet the needs of the environment. He advocated for recruiting new referees. Wu Bangwei seconded the proposal. Shao Leping, Chen Jixiang, He Chunhui, Wang Shifang, and others who attended the meeting agreed and passed the proposal. It will be handed over to the basketball committee of the association, Zhang Guoxun, Xu Zhendong, and Shu Hong, to actively handle. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Local News

Wu Tiecheng's Talk

Hoping the Whole Country Rises Up and Unites Against Foreign Aggression

The People on the Border Suffer Ten Times More Losses Than the Government

Dealing with the Russian Situation Based on the Declaration

The Candidates for Representatives Have Not Been Decided Yet

Wu Tiecheng, a member of the Central Supervisory Committee, returned to Shanghai by night train from Nanjing at 7:00 AM yesterday after completing his mission to the Northeast to comfort the soldiers fighting against Russia. Yesterday afternoon, a reporter from this newspaper interviewed him at his residence to inquire about the situation in the Northeast and the various aspects of the war negotiations. Wu's remarks are summarized as follows: Two Lessons Wu said, "I was ordered to go to the Northeast to comfort the soldiers fighting against Russia. After arriving in Liaoning, I originally planned to personally inspect the front lines, but at that time, Manzhouli and Hailar were invaded by Red Russia, and traffic west of Ang'angxi was cut off. I had no choice but to limit my trip to Qiqihar. I originally planned to visit the Xing'an Mountains, but I was unable to do so, which is a great regret." Wu also said, "Although we painfully conceded in this incident with Russia, we can learn two lessons: 1. Dealing with foreign affairs is not a local matter. The whole country should rise up and unite to resist foreign aggression. 2. From the Northeast to the Northwest, the border defense spans thousands of miles and has no defense. With the outer fences removed, we can only allow foreign invaders to slaughter us. We must find a way to remedy this situation as soon as possible."

Aftermath of the Northeast Incident Regarding the aftermath of the military situation in the Northeast, Wu said, "The Northeast authorities are now determined to find a way to recall the border guards and thoroughly replenish and reorganize them. As for the losses, the people on the border suffered ten times more than the government. The Northeast authorities are investigating and providing relief. The industry and commerce of the Northeast are still in their infancy, and the merchants and people on the border have a more rudimentary foundation. It is most heartbreaking that they have suffered such violence."

Negotiations with Russia Wu then said, "The records of the preliminary meeting in Boli contain many items that exceed the scope of the instructions from the National Government, such as the restoration of diplomatic relations and trade between the two countries. These issues should be discussed in another meeting. Therefore, the negotiations with Russia will be conducted entirely based on the declaration issued by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 8th. The official meeting will focus on discussing the aftermath of the China Eastern Railway issue and will not cover other matters. As for the candidates for representatives to the official meeting, they are currently being carefully considered."

The Third Plenary Session The Third Plenary Session is scheduled to be held on March 1st and is currently being actively prepared. Chairman Chiang's trip to Guangdong has been cancelled. It is not easy to determine whether he will be able to travel after the Third Plenary Session. He will rest in Shanghai for a few days before returning to Nanjing.

National General Chamber of Commerce Received Telegram from Ministry Yesterday

Regarding the Matter of Gold Price Hikes and Silver Price Declines

The National General Chamber of Commerce received a telegram from the Ministry of Industry yesterday, stating: "Shanghai Republic of China National General Chamber of Commerce, your telegram has been reviewed. It is noted that the recent surge in gold prices and decline in silver prices have suddenly created a tense situation in the financial market. The Ministry considers this to be of utmost importance to the future of our national economy. Previously, a telegram was sent to the Ministry's office in Shanghai, instructing them to convene a meeting with the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and the Chamber of Commerce to discuss relief measures, in order to gather diverse opinions. Furthermore, we received instructions from the government to consult with the Ministry of Finance. The proceedings of the meeting have been reported to the National Government for review. The consensus among the nation regarding relief measures for this financial crisis is to adopt the gold standard. However, encouraging production, reforming the monetary system, abolishing excessive taxes, facilitating transportation, and promoting domestic goods are all pressing priorities. The Ministry is currently drafting separate plans to be submitted for approval and implementation. The Chamber's telegram is insightful and pertinent, and its emphasis on restoring social and economic order and protecting public and private property is particularly profound and valuable for reference. You are instructed to continue monitoring the financial market situation at all times and report your findings for review. This is a special reply, Geng Yin (signature of) the Ministry of Industry."

Municipal Propaganda Department Expands Promotional Campaign for Domestic Goods

The campaign to promote domestic goods was originally decided by the Central Government as one of the seven major movements during the period of political tutelage for lower-level party branches. The Municipal Propaganda Department of this city held a large-scale domestic goods movement rally last year in conjunction with the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, which proved to be quite effective. Recently, the trend of expensive gold and cheap silver has erupted, which has a significant impact on the national economy and the people's livelihood. The department urgently ordered party branches at all levels to immediately engage in lectures and discussions, and instructed all party members to conduct practical research in order to remedy the situation. However, based on the current state of the nation, the people's livelihood, and the environment, the most urgent and fundamental solution is believed to be the promotion of domestic goods. On the one hand, this can reduce the losses caused by expensive gold and cheap silver, and on the other hand, it can revitalize industries, recover interests, and build the foundation of the national economy. Therefore, the department is sparing no effort in planning this movement. It is reported that they have already produced a promotional plan for the domestic goods movement, measures for holding lectures on the domestic goods movement, an outline of lecture materials for the domestic goods movement, and a brief overview of the impact of expensive gold and cheap silver. These four documents have been distributed to party branches at all levels and various public organizations to be followed for publicity purposes. In addition, a thick volume on the expensive gold and cheap silver crisis is currently being printed. This book contains a wealth of information and is a unique reference for studying this issue. It is expected to be published soon. It is reported that the department will set a date to convene a large-scale propaganda conference to expand the publicity. The aforementioned measures and outlines are summarized below:

Promotional Plan for the Domestic Goods Movement: ㈠ Regularly convene a propaganda conference for the domestic goods movement; ㈡ Party branches at all levels hold lectures on domestic goods; ㈢ Various public organizations hold lectures on domestic goods; ㈣ Organize lecture teams to promote domestic goods in various entertainment venues and factories (collect volunteers during district propaganda meetings, based on the principle of district allocation); ㈤ Invite experts to give lectures; ㈥ Formulate measures and reporting forms for party branches at all levels and public organizations to hold lectures on domestic goods, as well as lecture materials; ㈦ Write a report on the impact of expensive gold and cheap silver; ㈧ Request the Social Affairs Bureau to establish a domestic goods exhibition hall; ㈨ Request the Executive Committee to forward a request to the Central Government to issue a nationwide order that all party members and civil servants are prohibited from using foreign goods; ㈩ Request the Education Bureau to create permanent promotional lead skin slogans advocating the use of domestic goods and prohibiting the use of foreign goods. Made by the Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special City Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang.

Measures for Holding Lectures on the Domestic Goods Movement: ㈠ In order to enable all party members and people from all walks of life in the city to have a deep understanding of the significance and necessity of promoting domestic goods, and to implement the promotion, the Municipal Propaganda Department hereby orders party branches and public organizations at all levels to hold lectures on the domestic goods movement; ㈡ All district party branches, district sub-branches, and public organizations at all levels in the city must hold lectures; ㈢ When the meeting is held, all party members of party branches at all levels and all members of public organizations at all levels must attend; ㈣ The topics of the lectures will be determined and distributed by the Municipal Propaganda Department; ㈤ The lecture period will be from February 囗th and will last for 囗 weeks. During this period, each district sub-branch and public organization at all levels must hold at least two lectures; ㈥ The location and time of the meeting will be determined by each party branch or organization; ㈦ After the time and location of the meeting are determined, each party branch or organization must report to the Municipal Propaganda Department three days in advance so that personnel can be sent to participate and provide guidance; ㈧ The outline of lecture reference materials will be provided by the Municipal Propaganda Department, but each party branch or organization must also collect additional materials to enrich the content; ㈨ If anyone fails to comply with the regulations and hold the lectures within the specified time, the person in charge of the party branch or organization will be punished; ㈩ After each lecture, a written report must be submitted to the Municipal Propaganda Department for review. Made and printed by the Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special City Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang (19.2.7).

Outline of Lecture Materials for the Domestic Goods Movement: 　㈠ The significance of the domestic goods movement; ㈠ Promoting domestic goods is a key strategy to alleviate the crisis of expensive gold and cheap silver; ㈡ Promoting domestic goods is a way to support the weak and save the nation; ㈢ Promoting domestic goods is a plan for revenge and restoring national pride; ㈣ Promoting domestic goods is a policy of enriching the nation and benefiting the people; ㈤ Promoting domestic goods can promote the national spirit; ㈥ Promoting domestic goods can restore the inherent virtues of the nation; ㈦ History of the domestic goods movement; 　The economic invasion suffered by our country (A) The origin of economic invasion (B) The losses from foreign invasion (C) The losses from the invasion of foreign banks (D) The losses from concessions, land taxes, land rents, and land prices; (乙) The losses suffered by our country from the crisis of expensive gold and cheap money (A) Exchange rate losses, (甲) The impact of tariffs on domestic and foreign debt in terms of finance (乙) The losses of import merchants in commerce (B) Rising prices (甲) People's lives are difficult and society is uneasy; ㈢ History of boycotting foreign goods Road (B) Economic severance with Japan (A (boycott of British and American goods, ㈣ The reasons why domestic goods are not resisted and the principles of remedy (A) reasons, (甲) Lack of sustained spirit to resist foreign goods (乙) National taxes cannot be autonomous (丙) Imperialism is economically strong (丁) Domestic unrest is frequent; (戊) General domestic goods factories cannot be enterprising (己) Frequent labor unrest (A) Remedial principles (甲) Awaken the masses (乙) Fix the organization to promote domestic goods; (丙) Determine a plan to promote domestic goods, ㈢ Government measures that should be taken in the domestic goods movement ㈠ Implement protective tariffs, ㈡ Actively improve the tax system, ㈢ Reward the manufacture and improvement of domestic goods, ㈣ Cultivate and protect industrial talents ㈤ Promote the sales of domestic goods ㈥ Support agricultural and industrial production, abolish unequal treaties, ㈣ The efforts that the nation should make in the domestic goods movement, The basic conditions for the people of the whole country to promote domestic goods (A) Break the inferiority of superstitious foreign goods (B) Develop the habit of loving and using domestic goods, (C) Strive for economic severance with foreign countries ㈠ Entrepreneurs should take revitalizing industry and manufacturing domestic goods as their duty, ㈢ Merchants should absolutely refuse to sell counterfeit goods and sell domestic goods ㈣ Laborers should carefully study technology ㈤ Farmers, students and women should unanimously refuse to use foreign goods and vow to promote domestic goods as an example, ㈤ The methods of promoting domestic goods The government (B) the people (A) farmers (B) merchants (C) workers (D) students (E) women Made and printed by the Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special City Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang (19.17.)

Investigation Outline of the Impact of Expensive Gold and Cheap Silver:　Since our country implemented tariff autonomy and the call to abolish consular jurisdiction, it shocked the economic invading powers. Therefore, the imperialists, in panic, contacted each other and started from London and New York. With banks in China as tools, they tried their best to raise the price of gold, hoping to deprive our country of the ability of tariff autonomy, so that the economy would never be independent and they could cut and slaughter us. We know that this is indeed the final struggle of the great powers, and relying on our revolutionary diplomacy with the people of the whole country as our backing, we will eventually achieve our goal. However, the impact of this crisis has a great impact on the national economy and the people's livelihood, and it is really worth our understanding. The impact on finance is listed as follows: Expensive gold and cheap silver will lead to high water rates. High water rates will lead to increased pound losses. My country should pay a huge amount of compensation to foreign countries every year. According to the report of the General Tax Department, in the eighteenth year, 65,236,134.134 taels of standard silver were paid in principal and interest from tariffs, which was 7,947,388.54 taels more than the 57,388,724.87 taels in the seventeenth year. This is because the loss of pound loss due to the decline in money prices. Roughly every shilling shrinks by one penny, then China should pay 800,000 taels more in foreign debt, so if this continues, even if the tariff revenue is not reduced, the surplus due to the increase in the silver value of foreign debt will also become a problem. The surplus is the mortgage for domestic debt. If domestic and foreign debts lose their guarantee, the national finances will go bankrupt. The impact on the national economy is that, in terms of international trade, our country is a country that needs silver. The prices of all import and export goods often increase or decrease according to the exchange rate. Merchants are accustomed to valuing goods in gold coins when ordering, and the settlement is unclear. When the goods arrive in Shanghai, they are paid in silver. If the price of silver rises during this period, profits can be made. However, if the price of gold is high and the price of silver is cheap, the burden on merchants will be heavy, and they will lose their ability to settle and go bankrupt frequently. It is reported that the item of piece goods has not yet been settled at present, and the goods imported in February and March of last year have a huge amount of more than 20 million, and it seems that there has been no small loss in the recent situation. The price of gold is expensive, and the cost of imported finished goods or raw materials will also rise accordingly, so the goods in the domestic market will all rise in price. Rising prices will weaken the purchasing power of the people, and social life will immediately present a difficult phenomenon, and national wealth will be invisibly depleted. However, on the other hand, there is no small benefit for export merchants to drop the price of silver. The price of foreign goods is higher than that of domestic goods, and this can give us an opportunity to promote domestic goods. In fact, only by promoting domestic goods to balance imports and exports, and then achieve the goal of surplus can we save this current crisis, so I deeply hope that comrades and compatriots will unanimously advocate taking the lead in promoting domestic goods and working together to save the country. Made and printed by the Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special City Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang (19.2.7.)

Crisis of China's Tung Oil Industry

Britain Plans to Actively Try to Plant Tung Trees

London, 10th (Associated Press) - Since the invention of navigation, the tung oil industry has become increasingly important. Aircraft fuselages coated with tung oil will not be penetrated by moisture no matter how humid the climate is. Moisture is most taboo for aviation because it makes the machine heavier and is prone to rust. The world's supply of tung oil has always depended on China, but because China's sources are multiple provinces and have no fixed quantity, and orders often cannot be delivered on time, the world's tung oil market has felt the difficulty of supply falling short of demand. Since the European War, the United States has sought ways to produce tung trees in its own country, but the scope is too small. In view of this, Britain is now planning to actively try to plant tung trees to extract oil, with the intention of seizing this thriving new industry. The Kew Royal Botanic Gardens in Surrey, England, has been granted a special permit from the Bureau of Commerce, receiving a loan of US$3,500 to collect tung tree seeds and select land for planting. Such as Australia, New Zealand, South Africa, India, Burma, Ceylon, Essex, West Indies, Hong Kong, Malaysia, Palestine, etc., all of which are supplied with seeds by the botanical garden to carry out extensive trials, which are promising. In addition, the British Bureau of Commerce also plans to allocate a special fund of 3,750 yuan every year to the Paint Research Association to specialize in investigating places suitable for planting tung trees in the UK, testing planting, and the most economical method of extracting oil from oil seeds, and also on how to turn the oil residue into cake blocks for cattle and sheep feed.

The Municipal Government Revoked the Boat Donation Contractor

The boat donation in this city has always been contracted by merchants. The Land Bureau Handled the Oil Pond in Gaoqiao District

Land Bureau Director Zhu Yan reported to the Municipal Government, saying: "Report on the Da Hua Xingye Company purchasing land in Gaoqiao District from Yuxing Company and leasing it to the foreign merchant Asia Petroleum Company to build an oil pond. The bureau handled the collection of fees, and the situation of clearing and measuring is as follows, begging for your review and record. I am investigating the Da Hua Xingye Co., Ltd., which bought the land located in Gaoqiao District, Twenty-seventh Map, from Yuxing Company. On January 17, the Ministry of Finance Su Zi No. 27618, No. 27619, and No. 27620, with a total of 565 mu in the original amount, signed a contract in June 18. The Da Hua Company paid taxes to the Bureau on September 26, and paid 6 yuan of regular tax for every 100 yuan according to the contract price of 226,000 yuan, a total of 13,560 yuan, and 1 yuan of special construction donation, a total of 2,260 yuan. The handling fee was 271 yuan and 2 jiao, and the transfer fee was 300 yuan. The Bureau sent personnel to measure the land to be 529 mu, 1 fen, 4 li, and 7 hao. In addition to ordering the payment of 566 yuan for the measurement fee, since the land in the Ministry's license was only 167 mu, 1 fen, and 5 li, food had already been undertaken, and the rest had not yet been raised. The land that has not been raised should pay the land price and change the certificate and raise the food in accordance with the method of converting the land business license of the Ministry of Finance. According to the land contract price, each mu is 400 yuan, and 40% is paid. After deducting the 10 yuan per mu already paid as recorded in the Ministry's license, it is 49 mu, and each mu is 60 yuan, for a total of 313 mu. The company should pay an additional 38,650 yuan, which has also been ordered to pay in full in accordance with the regulations. This is the situation of the Bureau handling the sale, purchase, contract signing, clearing, measuring mu, collecting taxes and supplementary taxes, and paying the land price. Furthermore, this land was leased by the Chinese merchant Yuxing Company to the British merchant Asia Petroleum Company on January 23, 18 to build an oil pond. The lease was submitted to the Ministry of Agriculture and Minerals for approval, and was approved and recorded by the Asia Company on October 31, 18, ordering the Bureau to be informed. On the same day, the Asia Company and the Da Hua Xingye Co., Ltd. signed a lease transfer agreement, and submitted it to the Bureau for record. The Special City, the method of dividing the oil pond area, which was announced by the Bureau together with the Works Bureau, was on November 9, 18, so the special construction donation was not collected from the Asia Company in accordance with the method. This is the situation of the Asia Company renting the land and the Bureau not collecting the special construction donation in accordance with the newly established method. The above situation is compiled into a document for reporting, begging for your review and record. Sincerely submitted, "

Handling of Booth Locations in the City

Special Municipality Five-Bureau Joint Inspection Passed

Municipal Government Order Stipulating Measures Announced

Shanghai Special Municipality Mayor Zhang Qun, previously, due to the placement of stalls and vendors along roads and sidewalks in various streets and alleys of the city obstructing traffic, ordered a joint inspection by various bureaus. After the completion of the joint inspection by the Public Safety, Social Affairs, Finance, Public Works, and Health Bureaus, the Finance Bureau submitted a report to the Municipal Government, stating that it was a joint report matter. The Public Safety Bureau previously, due to the placement of stalls and vendors along roads and sidewalks in various streets and alleys of the city obstructing traffic, although repeatedly instructed the relevant district offices to strictly prohibit such activities, lacked corresponding measures. The donation permits held by the vendors only specified "a certain street" or "a certain road," without defining specific locations for setting up stalls, resulting in an increasing number of vendors crowding prosperous streets, arbitrarily arranging their goods, and causing disorder. Punishment in the morning was ineffective by evening, and strict prohibition and rectification were difficult to implement. Each district director was instructed to list the locations within their respective jurisdictions where stalls could be set up and where such activities should be prohibited, in order to formulate stall-setting measures. However, as this matter fell under the jurisdiction of various bureaus, a letter was sent to the Finance, Public Works, Social Affairs, and Health Bureaus, requesting them to send personnel to the Public Safety Bureau to hold the first meeting on prohibiting vendors from setting up stalls. A consensus was reached on the implementation plan, starting with the inspection of the area under the jurisdiction of the No. 1 District Office in Hu-Nan, followed by other district offices. During the inspection, the director of the relevant district office was responsible for guiding and first preparing a detailed list of the names and numbers of existing vendors within the area, in order to clearly identify locations and designate stall spaces. The locations for vendors to set up stalls were determined by drawing lots. After the resolution was passed, the Public Safety Bureau instructed the relevant district offices to comply, and at the same time, personnel from the Public Safety Bureau and the Finance Bureau were dispatched to inspect the areas under the jurisdiction of the First District and the Second Office in accordance with the plan. The inspection and determination of stall locations in various district offices and the handling of related matters are detailed below: (1) The inspection revealed that the streets inside and outside the Shiliupu area of the First District's jurisdiction were bustling with commercial activity, and the traffic of vehicles and pedestrians was often congested. The setting up of stalls and vendors had been prohibited by order. Although there were no longer any stalls in Shiliupu, the farmers now depended on the Farmers' Association of the First District for guidance. Now, with the New West District donation dispute pending for more than a year without resolution, and the South District righteousness in the south of Gaochang Temple not unified before the cleaning donation, Mo Baoquan also won the bid to undertake the project, but the farmers came out to obstruct it, and it could not be started and was interrupted. Therefore, it was not included in the unified donation. Now Longhua Town is even further south, and it is clearly impossible to organize before the New West District and the South District. It is obvious that the cleanliness of each place has long been manipulated and controlled by the Farmers' Association. Only by removing the knot can the problem be solved easily. If the two sides continue to hold on to each other, it will not be the end of the matter. Only by still asking for ways to strictly order the Farmers' Association to pay the New West District donation can we start from the South District and gradually move south to achieve unified results. Otherwise, it is impossible for merchants to bear the responsibility, which will only cause disputes and will not benefit the donation. It is reasonable to report the investigation and planning situation truthfully, and hope that the above information will be verified and forwarded. Based on this, the inspection and verification of the above-mentioned items are still the actual situation. It was also found that the case of the Farmers' Association of the First District refusing to pay the cleaning donation has been resolved after repeated meetings with the relevant bureaus by the bureau. The Gaochang District cleaning donation will be carried out according to the plan. In addition to waiting for the two cases to be completely concluded, the Longhua Town cleaning donation will be planned and organized and reported separately. The reason for the previous order is that it is reasonable to report first. I hope that the mayor will approve the report and then issue an order to the five bureaus: "The joint report and charts are all known. The temporary floating areas of the First District and the First District and Second Office, and the location of the small vegetable market, have been inspected and stipulated, and the handling has been standardized, and should be approved for record. The remaining district offices should expedite the implementation as soon as possible to achieve results as soon as possible. However, the location designated by each stallholder, if a stallholder closes down in the future due to various reasons, whether the site should be freely transferred to others, or should be reported to the relevant district offices when the stallholder closes down, and another new stallholder should be recruited, has not been stipulated. Future disputes are inevitable. You should take advantage of the initial handling of this matter, stipulate the measures uniformly, and announce them for implementation, so that there is a basis for compliance and to avoid disputes." This order.

Expansion of Sino-American Shipping Trend

Since the competition for silk cargo rates across the Pacific Ocean led to a reduction of one dollar per hundred pounds, Kawasaki Kisen Kaisha yesterday implemented the export of its Wales Maru, carrying 450 bales of silk bound for San Francisco and then transferred by rail to New York. Adding the railway transfer fee of nine dollars per bale, the total land and sea freight from Shanghai to New York for every hundred pounds of silk amounted to ten US dollars, reaching its destination in 23 days. After the rate reductions by major firms in this port such as Da Lai and Chang Xing, shipping via Seattle and Vancouver to the United States requires only 19 days to reach New York. However, this issue has caused great panic in the Sino-American shipping industry. There are more than ten shipping companies with New York lines owned by British, American, and Japanese merchants in Shanghai. Due to the competition for cargo from the Far East, each company built new ships last year. Since the disruption of silk cargo rates by Japanese merchants this time, each company also held an emergency meeting yesterday to discuss countermeasures. The fastest ships from Shanghai to New York take 36-37 days, which is two weeks longer than the Pacific route, but they can avoid the land transport fee. Considering the interest involved in the speed of cargo transport, the New York line ships held an alliance meeting and decided to reduce the fee for each bale of silk from Shanghai to New York by four US dollars (which is six dollars cheaper than the Pacific route with train freight). It was also decided to implement this from today to compete with the Pacific mail ships. This has further expanded the Sino-American shipping trend.

Navigation News from Beiyang

Last year, during the winter, the water in the Baihe River in Tianjin was shallow and frozen. Shanghai shipping companies could only transport goods to Tianjin to Dagu Port and then transfer them by barge. Therefore, a barge fee of five cents per item, such as grain, was charged. For goods such as foreign cloth, an additional barge fee of eight cents and four cents per ton was also charged. Recently, the water in the Baihe River has risen. Yesterday, Tianjin telegraphed that the river water was 18 feet deep and the ice had melted, and goods could enter the port. Therefore, the shipping companies announced that the barge fee would be canceled from today.

China-Japan Air Service Still Difficult to Achieve

No Scheduled Flights Allowed Before the Revision of the Sino-Japanese Treaty

The International Air Transport Company of Japan is actively preparing for the China-Japan international air transport planned. All procedures have been prepared and completed. It was originally scheduled to start trial flights on March 1 and officially fly on April 1. On the one hand, Acting Minister Shigetsu Aoi also instructed the Japanese Consul in Beijing, Uemura, to negotiate with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs nearby to request permission to fly. After repeated negotiations, there was no progress. The day before yesterday, Acting Minister Shigetsu had received formal notification from Foreign Minister Wang, that this scheduled international transport was related to the Sino-Japanese Commercial Treaty. Therefore, it was difficult to allow it before the Sino-Japanese New Treaty had been revised. It would be discussed together when the New Treaty was revised in the future. As for unofficial test flights, if the Ministry of Foreign Affairs approved them, they might be implemented. Therefore, the plan to implement scheduled flights has been suspended.

Municipal Government Prohibits Overstepping Authority to Interfere in Labor Disputes

The Municipal Government previously, according to the Social Bureau's request, prohibited any organizations from overstepping their authority to interfere in labor dispute events, in order to prevent disputes, etc. It is heard that the case has been approved by the mayor. In addition to sending separate letters to party and military agencies, a notice was issued to prohibit such interference. The notice stated, "For the matter of issuing a notice, according to the Social Bureau, the Labor Dispute Handling Law stipulates that the mediation agency for labor disputes is the administrative agency. The second article of the implementation rules of this law in this city stipulates that the administrative agency for mediating labor disputes is the bureau. It is obvious that the authority to mediate labor disputes in this city belongs to the bureau. However, party and military agencies at all levels in this city often overstep their authority to interfere in labor disputes. Even the General Labor Union, which has not yet been established, also sent personnel to freely mediate labor disputes, resulting in confusion of authority and even more disputes. If such interference is not prevented early, it is feared that many malpractices will arise, which would be a disaster for both labor and management. It is reasonable to prepare a document and request that you respectfully review and issue a strict notice prohibiting any organizations from overstepping their authority to interfere in labor dispute events, in order to prevent disputes and benefit mediation, which is in the public interest." Based on this, it is natural to approve the claim that the above-mentioned claim is for the purpose of strictly complying with laws and regulations and avoiding confusion of authority and the generation of malpractices. In addition to sending separate letters to party and military agencies for investigation and prevention, a notice must be issued to the effect that, in the event of labor disputes in the city, they must be submitted to the competent authorities for handling in accordance with the law. No organization may overstep its authority to interfere, so as to clarify its authority and comply with laws and regulations. Be sure to publish this.
