The above, except for Buick, Nash, and Chrysler, all include trucks. And among them, eight types are American goods, two are British goods, two are French goods, and one is Italian goods. Therefore, it can be seen that most of the automobiles in this city are made in the United States. This is because American cars accelerate very quickly, are long and wide, and have large cylinders. Although other countries are trying to imitate them, people from various countries still mostly purchase American cars. However, most of the motorcycles in this city are made in the United Kingdom.

Although the number of automobiles increases every year, this year is not optimistic. Due to the recent impact of the high price of gold and the low price of silver, the original price of automobiles must increase by at least 20%.

A General Discussion of the German Automobile Industry by Huang Yingdai

Recently, the automobile industries of various European countries have been competing fiercely with the United States. This is something that everyone knows. Among the various European countries, the German automobile industry has also been developing rapidly in recent years. And the recent business policies of German automobile factories are focused on improving the quality of their products to prevent the import of foreign automobiles. According to a German newspaper, the total number of imported foreign automobiles in April and May of last year was 2,526, with a value of 7,574,000 marks. In April and May of 1928, the number of imported automobiles was 3,636, with a value of 14,685,000 marks. In comparison, it can be seen that the import of German automobiles decreased significantly last year compared to the previous year. According to customs reports, the number of automobiles imported last year was only one-third of the previous year. The rest were all bodies and chassis. On the other hand, in the first four months of last year, the import of domestic automobiles was 37,997, while in the same period of 1928, it was only 25,394. It can be seen that the sales of German automobiles in recent years have not declined, but have been developing year by year. However, the import of foreign automobiles will gradually decrease. This is also sufficient evidence of the development of German domestic products. However, most German automobile factories have foreign investment. For example, General Motors and Ford have branches in Germany. Therefore, in reality, although German automobile factories have been developing rapidly in recent years, a portion of their rights have still been seized by foreigners.

The German automobile industry is as described above, and the German motorcycle industry has also been gradually developing recently. This is because the German people have recently been fond of riding motorcycles, so the production of motorcycles has also been increasing day by day. According to the report of Vossiche Zllung in Berlin, the total number of motorcycles produced by German factories in the six months from January to June of last year was 115,000, while in the six months from January to June of the previous year, it was only 70,000. The difference is more than one-third. Moreover, Germans prefer to ride small motorcycles, so the motorcycles produced by various factories have recently adopted a policy of producing mostly small-sized motorcycles in order to cater to social psychology and make them easier to sell. For example, the Opel factory and other automobile factories all adopt this policy. As for large motorcycles with a price of more than US$500, a total of 41,500 were produced in the six months from January 1st to July 1st of last year, a decrease of 10% compared to the same period in 1928. On the other hand, when Germans buy motorcycles, they recently prefer to choose those priced from 75 to 150 yuan. Therefore, the production of small motorcycles has suddenly increased in recent years. The production in the past two years has increased tenfold compared to 1927. How can we not be surprised when we hear this? The registration of German motorcycles ranks second in the world in terms of quantity. As of January 1, 1929, the total number of motorcycle registrations in various countries was 724,830 in the United Kingdom, 465,000 in Germany, 320,000 in France, and 121,656 in the United States. Therefore, Germany is the most numerous except for the United Kingdom.

One country that has been affected by the development of the German automobile industry is Poland. And the speed of the promotion of the public bus industry in Poland is particularly surprising. According to the survey by the American Polish Chamber of Commerce, Poland had only 412 public buses in 1925, but now there are 2,900. Among them, the majority are made in the United States. In addition to Warsaw, major Polish cities and towns, such as Popnan, Lwow, Cracow, Wilna, Lublin, Cpesochowg, and Binlystolk, all have public bus lines. Travelers in rural towns can take buses everywhere. The convenience of transportation is self-evident. Moreover, these bus lines are connected to various railways. The total number of passengers carried daily is as high as 168,000, while the number of passengers on trains is only one-third of that.

The Ford Car of the Long March by Lin

Bearing Heavy Burdens and Achieving Distant Goals is Rare

The Dearborn Ford Motor Company has received reports from all over the world praising the excellent quality and outstanding performance of the new Ford cars. Recently, in the [Travel Competition] held by the De Vie Yuk Automobile Club in Kalia’s Skitte City, Ford cars won the first and fifth prizes. The other three prizes were won by non-American made cars. The route of this competition was unprecedented. The path used to be taken by riders, so both the drivers and the car bodies bore heavy burdens. The entire ground was rugged and uneven, with ponds and swamps, making it extremely uneven and difficult to drive. There were also stop signs at any time in the middle of the journey, unexpectedly causing the cars to stop. The cars participating in the competition had to brake at any time.

The winner of the first prize was the car driven by Paul Saxes, with the highest score of 1,097 points. The second prize was 1,079 points, the third prize was 1,054 points, the fourth prize was 1,048 points, and the fifth prize was also won by a Ford car with 1,045 points. Last autumn in July, in the Xinaru local area of Finland, Ford cars won prizes in six out of seven competitions. The competition site was near the Gulf of Bosnia. All types of cars participating in the competition were standard models. The only competition that the Ford drivers did not participate in was the fifth. During the second competition, the path was 10 kilometers long. The participants all maintained neat sports cars. The prize was won by a Ford car. This car had also participated in the first competition, only the windshield was removed and slightly changed.

Among the owners of Ford Model A cars, the long-distance travel report made by Li Honglangmei, a securities dealer from Brooklyn, New York, is the most interesting. Lang drove his sedan Ford car, starting from the city and heading to the West Coast. The speedometer on his car only had 90 miles, but before returning, this car had traveled as many as 8,709 miles. There were four passengers on board, weighing more than 680 pounds, and four large luggage boxes were loaded in the back of the car, not counting the miscellaneous items.

Langmei said in a letter, [We traveled 8,709 miles, passing through all the best and worst roads. But this car can cross any mountain and travel on any road. As for the changes in weather, there are not many problems for this car. We entered and exited the snow in Burk Mountain and the unbearably hot Mahahe River desert. When we reached the New Mexico border, it rained heavily, almost every night. The roads were washed away by the rain, but our car was still able to cross them. The only difference was that the mud overturned the car body, leaving a mud print in the engine. The car traveled through Yellowstone Park, Peach McToth, McLeabyss, Glerough Lake, Daka Rong, Cliff De Wheeler, Color Desert, Penderfet, Flayest, and major cities such as Old Mountain, Los Angeles, St. Louis, Kansas City, and Portland, etc.]

In addition to the above-mentioned 8,709-mile long-distance journey, there is also the long-distance automobile journey of engineer Maggen from Cape Town, Africa, and his wife. The entire route traveled was 7,500 miles. Mr. and Mrs. Maggen went deep into the interior of South Africa for as long as fourteen weeks. Mr. Maggen’s mode of transportation for this trip was a Ford truck. According to Mr. Maggen, the long march of thousands of miles was almost unpredictable. His wife was the only white woman who went deep into this dangerous place. The encounters and sights were bizarre and indescribable. The most difficult thing in the whole journey was the excessive heat, which was scorching and unbearable. The temperature rose to 125 degrees at sunrise and was still around 52 degrees at sunset. Fresh food would spoil in a short time. The only thing they could rely on to survive was canned food.

Recent Conditions of Zhejiang Highways by Yang Xiufan

My uncle works at the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau. Last year, I happened to go to Hangzhou for business and stayed at the bureau for several nights. As a result, I learned a lot about the recent conditions of the various lines under the jurisdiction of the Provincial Highway Bureau. I will now describe them below.

(1) Xiaoshao Section: This is one section of the Zhejiang-Fujian trunk line in the former Zhejiang Provincial Road Bureau's plan. It starts from Jiangbian Station on the south bank of the Qiantang River and ends at Wuyunmen in Shaoxing, connecting to the privately-run Shao Cao Sheng Automobile Road. The entire road is 90 li long. It passes through Xixing, Xiaoshan, Zhuanbatou, Yinlongzha, Yaqian, Qianqing, Qinwang, Ruanshe, Keqiao, Zunyiqiao, Xiguomen, Shaoxing, Changanmen, and other stations before reaching Wuyunmen. Each trip takes about two hours, and the fare is 1.2 yuan. There are a total of 30 round trips per day. There are also sectional buses between other stations, just like the regulations for trains. The total daily revenue of passenger tickets and luggage at all stations on the entire road averages more than 2,000 yuan. The average total number of passengers per day is more than 1,400. This road is an important route for travel between Hangzhou and Shaoxing. Travelers who choose to travel by land all take buses. Therefore, travelers rush to fill the stations, like a tidal wave. When the buses depart, they connect several vehicles, and there are no empty seats. Therefore, it is the most developed of all roads in the province.

(2) Gongsan Section: This is one section of the Hangshao Line. It was built in the autumn of the 17th year of the Republic of China (1928). It starts from Gongchen Bridge and ends at Sanlangmiao Station on the bank of the Qiantang River. It passes through Xiaohe, Guanyinqiao, Wulinmen, West Main Street, Hubin Road, Yongjinmen, Qingbomen, and Fengshanmen. The entire road is 24 li long. It imitates the public buses in Shanghai, and tickets are purchased on the bus. Buses depart three times per hour. The highest ticket price is 3.2 jiao, and the rest are in the range of a few fen. However, the average daily operating income is always more than 200 or 300 yuan. This road connects Ning, Shao, and Jinqu in the north, and connects to the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway in the south. Therefore, there are many travelers coming and going. If the equipment is complete in the future, it can be operated safely.

(3) Yin Feng Line: This is part of the Zhejiang coastal line. In the future, it will connect to the Shao Cao Highway in the west to reach Hangzhou. It will cross Pingyang in the south and reach Fuding in Fujian Province, becoming the eastern thoroughfare between Zhejiang and Fujian provinces. The section from Ningbo to Xikou in Fenghua (the hometown of Mr. Chiang Kai-shek) is 61 li long. It started operating in June of this year. The road passes through Duntang, Shiqi, Lishe, Hengzhang, Qianwang, Jiangkou, Dabu, Qishan, and other places. The buses make a total of 16 round trips per day and take about one hour. The passenger ticket price is 8 jiao. The scenery along the entire road is quite good, and the business is fairly developed.

(4) Hangchang Road: This is part of the Ninghang National Highway. This road goes from Hangzhou, through Liangzhu, Pingyao, Wukang, Wuxing, and Changxing, and reaches the Father and Son Ridge on the border of Jiangsu Province. It is 245 li long in total. The currently operating sections are the Hangzhou to Moganshan section and the Hangzhou to Huzhou section. The Hangzhou to Moganshan section is 114 li long. It starts from the city station and passes through Hubin, Wulinmen, Xiaohe, Penggongling, Shangbai, Wukang, Sanqiaobu, and reaches Moganshan Station. The passenger ticket price is 1.23 yuan. The Hanghu section also starts from the city station, reaches Wukang, and passes through Daixi, Qingshan, and Shijiaqiao before reaching Huzhou. The entire journey is 170 li long, and the fare is 2.21 yuan. In the future, after the entire road is directly connected, the development of business prospects is immeasurable.

The above-mentioned roads are all highways that belong to the Provincial Highway Bureau and have already been opened to traffic. Other roads that have been completed and will be opened to traffic, as well as privately-run automobile roads, could not be mentioned. From this, it can already be seen that the Zhejiang provincial authorities have made rapid progress in road renovation and construction in recent years.

Miscellaneous Records

Overview of Road Administration in Gansu Province: Enlightenment and Non-Belief

Gansu Province is remotely located in the Northwest, with overlapping mountains and ridges. The opening and management of roads is particularly crucial. Bordering Shaanxi and Shanxi to the east and Xinjiang and Mongolia to the north, traffic is frequent, and the transport of goods requires good transportation. If roads are not built, it is difficult to achieve results. An investigation reveals that there are eight major road lines which have been completed or are in the process of completion, all with Lanzhou in Gansu Province as the central hub. The function of these roads is divided into two types: motor vehicle roads and railways. About five thousand *li* of roads are already open to traffic. These are described separately below.

(1) Lanzhou-Pingliang Line: From Lanzhou to Pingliang, and then to Changwu in Shaanxi, connecting with the Shaanxi motor vehicle road. The road has been completed and open to traffic for a long time. However, the gradients along the route are still not ideal and are being diligently reduced section by section. The bridges that have been completed are in the counties of Pingliang, Guyuan, Zhuanglang, Jingning, Dingxi, and Hening. In Gaolan, there are six large and small bridges, and in Qiao Zhong, there are nine large and small bridges. The main road has been completely constructed and leveled, and is inspected and repaired as necessary. The bridges are also under construction.

(2) Lanzhou-Ningxia Line: From Lanzhou to Ningxia Province and then to Dengkou. The old motor vehicle road route goes from Lanzhou through Changliushui in Jingyuan, crossing the Yellow River twice, avoiding the sand dunes, to Zhongwei and then to Dengkou. This has long been open to traffic. However, due to the obstruction of the sand dunes, traffic is inconvenient. The route has been changed to go through Jingyuan, Bieduzi, Shuiquan, Dahonggou, Baiquanzi, Sikouzi, Ninganpu, to Zhongwei. This section of the project is currently 84 *li* and has not yet been completed. The rest is constructed smoothly. As for bridges, in Jingyuan and Gaolan, the roads are flat and there is no need to build them. The main road has also been completely constructed and leveled.

(3) Lanzhou-Suzhou Line: From Lanzhou to Suzhou, and then to Yumen, connecting to Xinjiang. A branch line from Gaotai goes to Mao Mu in Inner Mongolia. The Anxi-Mao Xiu branch line goes to Dunhuang. The main motor vehicle road from Lanzhou to Suzhou and the branch line from Gaotai to Mao Mu in Inner Mongolia have been completed. The branch line from Anxi to Dunhuang is still under construction. The Lanzhou-Suzhou railway has been fully completed. Because this line has no major rivers, there are no major bridge projects.

(4) Lanzhou-Huangyuan Line: From Lanzhou to Qinghai Province. The motor vehicle road within Gansu has been completed but is being improved. The section within Qinghai Province is mostly stone road, and discussions are underway with the Qinghai provincial government to excavate it. As for the motor vehicle bridge on the Yellow River in Xincheng, Gaolan County, a pontoon bridge has been erected and a ferry is in operation. The railway has been completed and is in operation, but the section within Qinghai Province still needs to be organized.

(5) Lanzhou-Qinzhou Line: From Lanzhou to Tianshui, divided into east and west lines. The east line motor vehicle road runs parallel to the Lanzhou-Pingliang road to Tongwei and Huajialing, then diverges to Tianshui. This has now been completed, and the bridges have all been erected. The west line motor vehicle road goes from Didao through Longxi to Dashui. This line is mountainous and rugged, and excavation will take time. It is currently being surveyed. The main roads on both the east and west lines have been repaired and are now open to traffic.

(6) Lanzhou-Hezhou Line: From Lanzhou to Daohe, divided into east and west lines. The west line motor vehicle road goes from Gaolan Xixiang, through Lianhuacheng to Daohe. This line has been completed and open to traffic for a long time. The east line motor vehicle road shares the same route as the Lanzhou-Qinzhou west line to Didao, then diverges. It is currently being surveyed.

(7) Lanzhou-Xuyuan Line: From Lanzhou to Xuyuan, connecting to the Ningxia-Pingliang road. The motor vehicle road shares the same route as the Lanzhou-Ningxia road to Jingyuan and Bieduzi, then diverges, passing through Yanchi County, to Xuyuan. The entire road has been completed and open to traffic, but the Dalachi section in Jingyuan is being repaired.

(8) Ningxia-Pingliang Line: This line does not start from Lanzhou, but from Ningxia to Pingliang. The construction and opening of the motor vehicle road has been in place for a long time, and only requires occasional repairs. The bridges and the railway have all been completed and are open to traffic.

The above eight lines are the most recently constructed and opened roads in Gansu Province, which are beneficial for transportation and convenient for commerce. The benefits are not superficial. Even the people of Inner Mongolia and Xinjiang are more receptive to Han Chinese culture, which is also due to these several roads, allowing them to travel back and forth. The completed mileage of motor vehicle roads in Gansu Province are all dirt roads, with a width of 25 *chi*. The Lanzhou-Pingliang road from Lanzhou to Jingzhou Yaodian is 1200 *li* and has been open to traffic for a long time. The Lanzhou-Ningxia road from Lanzhou to Baiquanzi in Haiyuan is 627 *li* and is also open to traffic. The Lanzhou-Suzhou road from Lanzhou to Dingxin County is 1450 *li* and is open to traffic. The Lanzhou-Qinzhou road from Lanzhou to Qingshui is 720 *li* and is open to traffic. The Lanzhou-Huangyuan road from Lanzhou to the Pingfan border is 390 *li* and is not yet open to traffic. The Lanzhou-Xuyuan road from Lanzhou to Xuyuan is 770 *li* and is open to traffic. The Ningxia-Pingliang road from Zhongjie to Pingliang is 450 *li* and is open to traffic. The Lanzhou-Hezhou road from Lanzhou to Daohe is 300 *li* and is also open to traffic. Therefore, considering the mileage of the eight lines, the roads already open to traffic cover more than 5000 *li*.

Motor Vehicle Transportation as a Source of National Wealth - Auspicious Person

The United States has always been known as a prosperous and strong nation, with developed industry and commerce, and excellent products. People from all countries regard it as a land of wealth, and tens of thousands go there every year to do business. Recently, overseas commercial magnates and bankers have organized inspection teams to go to the United States to investigate the reality of industrial development, and to offer the results to their home countries to engage in the improvement of industry and commerce and revitalize industry.

Today, the governments of Europe, Australia, and the Far East are paying close attention to the automobile industry and its tax system in the United States. They have also selected commissioners to go to the United States to conduct inspections, with the aim of developing national roads and automobile transportation.

Officials who have inspected the United States and ladies who have traveled around the continent all say that the greatness of the American automobile industry is closely related to the country's wealth. The total amount of American investment in the automobile industry is 30 billion US dollars. The annual output value is about 50 billion US dollars or more. There are also 4 million men and women workers in various factories. The scale of the American automobile industry is rarely seen in the world. Americans have a considerable understanding of automobile transportation. The convenience of transportation is related to the prosperity or decline of the country, the progress of society, and the development of the economy, all of which are greatly affected. The current trend in North America is to expand national roads and connect the states, so that the people can share the benefits and everyone can own a car.

The development of automobile transportation has greatly facilitated commercial business. However, there will be a huge loss in railway revenue. Freight cars and buses are cheap and fast, convenient and comfortable, far better than trains. As a result, more and more people are using automobiles. Trains are lacking passengers. The railway is suffering from this unlimited competition, and business is becoming increasingly depressed. Tax revenue has been greatly reduced. As a result, several countries have risen up to find ways to rescue them. They ordered Congress to enact legislation to levy heavy taxes on the automobile industry to restore railway business, such as increasing the government's original tax rate.

The trend in the United States is different. Today's new and sensitive methods of transportation are warmly welcomed. Even railway companies use freight cars to carry goods for short distances. They also use buses to pick up and drop off passengers and load and unload luggage. The government does not issue laws to hinder it, but instead strives to promote and advocate it. Therefore, the breadth of American avenues, the number of vehicles, the convenience of transportation, and the prosperity of business are by no means comparable to other countries.

American road vehicle companies are indeed unable to compete with automobiles, but they are still working hard to maintain their business or switch to using automobiles. According to the results, the benefits of the automobile industry exceed the profits of other vehicle industries several times. This is the reason why the American automobile industry is so developed.

Today, the US federal government, in view of the need for roads, has distributed huge sums of money to the states to build and repair avenues. In addition, each state has a long-term road construction fee, which is drafted by the provincial government and then paid after being resolved by Congress.

Road construction policy is related to local security, industrial and commercial development, and many benefits. It can be compiled into a thick book. Take the farmers as an example. The roads are open, the transportation of goods is convenient, and the benefits are abundant. In terms of business, the value of land along the roads increases, and the profit from goods is ten times higher.

After the fact-finding missions and commissioners from various countries conducted on-the-spot investigations of the current situation of transportation in the United States, they concluded that the prosperity and strength of the United States is entirely dependent on the development of automobile transportation. When they return to their countries in the future to promote the automobile industry, they will surely make great contributions.

The initial concept of Americans regarded automobiles as consumables and luxury goods, which ordinary people could not afford. In recent years, people have deeply understood the benefits of automobiles and the economy of their use. Their attitude has changed dramatically. Everyone is buying cars. Therefore, the total number of vehicles in the United States today has reached more than five million.

The American automobile industry will surely be more revitalized in the future. With urban transformation and increased roads, the sales of automobiles will surely increase rapidly.

The General Motors Manufacturing Plant in the United States is the largest automobile manufacturer in the world. Its capital is 4 billion US dollars. It has 4 million workers. It has 24 branches in various countries. The output is large, the materials are beautiful, the parts are strong, and the sales are the widest. It can meet the needs of the global automobile industry. Therefore, the service of the General Motors Manufacturing Plant in the United States is the most satisfactory and is recognized by the world.
